> 4130:"Legendary Enchantment\nThis effect never expires, recast the spell to toggle the effect.\nInfuse your body with power, causing each Glint Sorcery you cast to increase the damage of Glint Sorceries by 1%. This effect stacks up to nine times. \nWhen you cast your tenth Glint Sorcery, all previous stacks are canceled and you gain a buff for 30 seconds. \nThat buff increases the damage of all Glint Sorceries by 15%, reduces the FP cost of sorceries by 20%, grants 20 FP regeneration per second and you gain additional poise. \nWhile this effect is active, you cannot gain stacks.\n\nThis spell is in essence the perfected form of what both Master Lusat and Master Azur were pursuing, a pure infusion of glintstone into the body and therefore a method of channeling the primeval current directly into sorceries. \nWhile the old masters' efforts ultimately fell short, such a technique would never be possible without their sacrifice.\n"

= 4130:"传说中的法术\n此效果永不过期，再次施法以开关效果。\n给身体注入力量，每施放一个辉石魔法攻击力提升1%，此效果最多可叠加9次。\n当你施放第10次辉石魔法时，之前所有的伤害叠加将被取消并获得一个持续30秒的Buff。\n该Buff提升15%辉石魔法攻击力，降低20%魔法专注值消耗，每秒获得20点专注值回复，并获得额外的强韧度。\n当此Buff有效时，你无法进行伤害叠加。\n\n本质上，这一法术乃是卢瑟特与亚兹勒两位大师所追求的完美形式——将辉石力量完全注入身体的方法，因此亦是将起源直接引入魔法的方式。\n虽然年迈大师们的努力以失败告终，但若没有他们的牺牲，这样的技艺也不可能得以实现。"

= 4560:"一种引导龙人力量的魔法。\n\n释放一些冰雷箭，从上方攻击并向外扩散，对敌人造成伤害并累积冻伤量表。"
> 4570:"A master level sorcery of the underworld.\nConjure a number of large bubbles that float upward and then burst and rain down frozen lightning upon enemies. Charging causes tendrils of lightning to erupt near where the downpour strikes and spread out in all directions."
= 4570:"地下世界的大师级法术。\n召唤出许多大泡泡，随后会爆炸，将冰雷倾泻到敌人身上。蓄力会在倾泻处附近炸开雷电流，并向四周扩散。"
> 4580:"A sorcery of the artificial denizens of the underworld.\nLegendary Enchantment\nWhile active, increases all weapon damage by 10%, reduces weapon stamina consumption by 20% and increases all absorption by 20%. Reduces total FP by 50% and reduces all spell damage by 20%.\n\nEffect never expires. Recast the spell to toggle the effect."
= 4580:"地底人造居民的魔法。\n传说中的法术\n激活时，提升10%武器攻击力，降低20%武器精力消耗，提升20%减伤率，降低50%最大专注值和20%法术攻击力。\n\n效果永不过期。再次施法以开关效果。"
> 4581:"A sorcery of the artificial denizens of the underworld.\nLegendary Enchantment\nWhile active, increases total FP by 20%, adds additional FP regeneration of 2 per second and increases spell damage by 10%. Reduces total HP by 30% and decreases all weapon damage by 50%.\n\nEffect never expires. Recast the spell to toggle the effect."
= 4581:"地底人造居民的魔法。\n传说中的法术\n激活时，提升20%最大专注值，额外提升2点每秒专注值回复，并提升10%魔法攻击力。减少30%最大精力和最大血量，降低50%武器攻击力。\n\n效果永不过期。再次施法以开关效果。"
> 4590:"A Sorcery that channels the power of the Dragonkin Soldiers.\n\nEnchants armaments held in the right hand with the power of frozen lightning, adding lightning damage and causing frost build-up on any foe struck by the weapon. Lasts for 60 seconds."
= 4590:"一种引导龙人力量的魔法。\n\n使右手握持的武器具有冰雷的力量，增加雷属性攻击力，并对该武器击中的敌人累积冻伤量表。持续60秒。"
> 4601:"A sorcery of the night maidens of the Nox.\n\nFires a projectile that applies a poison of life-sapping silver, dealing damage to the target slowly over 10 seconds.\n\nOften used to assist in assassination, the night maidens employed many forms of silver-based toxins. This does not stack with other quicksilver spells."
= 4601:"诺克斯黑夜女巫的魔法。\n\n释放一枚飞弹，释放出致命的水银毒素，在10秒内对目标缓慢造成伤害。\n\n黑夜女巫会使用多种形式的水银毒素，常常用于协助暗杀。这一法术不能与其它水银法术叠加。"
> 4602:"A secret sorcery of the ancient Nox empire.\n\nFires a projectile that causes a curse on impact. The curse lowers the target’s absorption to magic damage by 10% and slowly drains the target’s HP over 25 seconds.\n\nThis skill was reserved only for Nox assassins that had undergone the ritual of darkness. A practice which was said to elicit absolute loyalty to the empire for those that participated in it.\nThis ritual was considered barbaric by the conclave of night maidens, who valued free will among the peoples of their society."
= 4602:"古老诺克斯帝国的秘密魔法。\n\n释放能在击中时造成诅咒的飞弹。诅咒降低目标10%魔力属性减伤率，并在25秒内缓慢消耗目标的血量。\n\n这一技艺只传授给经受过黑暗仪式的诺克斯刺客。据说，这一仪式能够确保参与者对帝国的绝对忠诚。\n黑夜女巫议会视此为野蛮之举，她们尤为重视族人的自由意志。"
> 4603:"A sorcery of the night maidens of the Nox.\n\nLaunches a projectile from a distance removed from the caster, so as to strike the enemy from behind. When struck, enemies are afflicted with a quicksilver poison, which slowly drains HP.\n\nThis spell was the result of a collaboration with the night maidens and the assassins, combining shard tactics and life-sapping silver. This does not stack with other quicksilver spells."
= 4603:"诺克斯黑夜女巫的魔法。\n\n从远离施法者的距离发射飞弹，从后面攻击敌人。被击中时，敌人会受到水银毒素的影响，并慢慢消耗血量。\n\n这一法术是刺客和黑夜女巫合作的结果，融合了魔砾战术与缓慢剥夺生命的水银。此法术不能与其它水银法术叠加。"
< 4620:"One of the night sorceries of Sellia, Town of Sorcery.\n\nFires a semi-invisible magic comet.\nThis sorcery can be cast repeatedly and while in motion. Charging enhances potency.\n\nThe Sellian sorcerers were assassins, and it is said that they often hunted their fellows."
> 4620:"One of the night sorceries of the ancient Nox empire.\n\nFires a dark magic comet.\nThis sorcery can be cast repeatedly and while in motion. Charging enhances potency.\n\nAs night shard sorceries became more advanced, many of the assassins of the Nox began to move away from close quarters assassinations, instead preferring to stay out of reach while dispatching their targets.\nThese assassins are often regarded as the first of the oracle sect, the closest analog the Nox ever had to a traditional sorcerer."

= 4620:"古代诺克斯帝国的黑夜魔法之一。\n\n发射一颗黑暗魔法彗星。\n这个魔法可以走动释放，也可以重复释放。蓄力增强威力。\n\n随着黑夜魔砾法术日益进步，许多诺克斯刺客不再进行近身暗杀，而倾向于呆在难以触及的地方迅速处置目标。\n这些刺客常被视作第一批神谕官——诺克斯帝国中最接近传统魔法师的人。"

> 4672:"A sorcery of the oracles of the nameless eternal city.\nLegendary Enchantment\nIncreases FP regeneration by 5 per second, adds 20 HP regeneration per second, lowers the FP cost of sorceries by 50% and makes the caster less likely to stagger but reduces all damage you deal by 75%.\nEffect never expires. Recast the spell to toggle the effect.\n\nThe black moon was once the living deity of the Nox. Floating suspended above their unnamed city, it was the source of their strength and devotion. The moon itself acted as a window to the bottomless power of the primeval current and channeled that power throughout the empire.\nIt was the Nox oracles who developed the practice of phasing their own bodies partially into the primeval current. A skill thought to be unobtainable since the fall."

> 4820:"One of the sorceries developed from the magma of Mt. Gelmir.\n\nFires a lump of condensed magma that deals damage after hitting the target. = 4820:"格密尔的其中一种熔岩魔法。\n\n能释放命中敌人后会造成伤害的紧致熔岩飞弹。如果熔岩击中地面，短暂延迟后会引起爆炸，对周围的敌人造成更大的伤害。\n借由蓄力能发射三枚熔岩飞弹。\n\n蕾娜菈女王的子嗣拉卡德，\n成功让格密尔的古老咒术以魔法姿态重见天日。"

= 4840:"大蛇的毁灭性招式。\n\n用岩浆在你面前撕裂大地。借由蓄力能提升威力。\n\n格密尔火山的大蛇将岩浆的热量视作一种养分，滋养祂成为比肩神祇的存在。对受难者释放力量时，祂既展现了对这些弱小生物的蔑视，却也希望终有一天能碰到对等的存在——能与其一道在火焰中狂欢的存在。"

> 4852:"A sorcery of Rykard, Lord of Blasphemy.\nLegendary Enchantment\nGain an effect that adds 1% additional HP, FP and SP and 1% additional damage every time an enemy dies. This ability stacks up to 10 times.\nEffect never expires, recast the spell to toggle the effect.\n\nIn Rykard’s quest to achieve a strength to rival the power of the Erdtree, he would sacrifice his very humanity and allow himself to be consumed by the great serpent. In his view, this was not a sacrifice but rather a stepping stone to a god-like state. In this form he would hope to wield both the power of the serpent and also the combined strength of all the souls he had consumed. However, what he could not foresee was that his own desire for supremacy would be replaced with the serpent’s desire to consume all things. And thus, in body and mind, he was utterly lost."
= 4852:"“亵渎君王”拉卡德的魔法。\n传说中的法术\n获得一个效果，每次敌人死亡时额外提升1%血量, 专注值和精力以及1%额外伤害，此技能最多可叠加10次。\n效果永不过期，重放该法术以开关该效果。\n\n为获得与黄金树抗衡的力量，拉卡德牺牲自己的人性，放任自己被大蛇吞噬。在他看来，这不是牺牲，而是通往近神之道的基石。以这种形态，他既能运用蛇的力量，又能融合被吞噬的所有灵魂的力量。然而，他不曾预见，自己渴望达成至高的欲望会被蛇吞噬一切的欲望取代。因此，他的身心完全迷失了。"

= 4951:"来自几乎被遗忘的欧赫的魔法。\n\n召唤一把红色的念动巨剑，然后发起横扫攻击，发射出红色的刀刃，对敌人造成伤害并积累出血量表。可以重复释放。\n释放后会对自己积累出血异常量表。\n\n欧赫勇士艾梅隆尔是许多源自恐怖鲜血星星的异端技艺的保管人。"
> 4960:"An aberrant sorcery of those branded as guilty.\nPerpetual Enchantment\nConjure a floating red orb above your head that provides light, increases all physical damage you deal by 5% and grants 2 HP recovery per second.\n\nThis effect never expires, recast the spell to toggle the effect.\n\nThe eye of the dreaded Blood Star. Only conjured by those locked into eternal darkness, this totem’s gift is that of sight reborn. This vision is tainted with malice and hunger, it shows a world of victims and is driven by an endless drive toward predation.\n"
= 4960:"有罪之人的异端魔法。\n永久性法术\n在头顶释放一个漂浮的红色球体，照亮周围，提升5%物理攻击力，每秒恢复2点血量。\n\n此效果永不过期，再次施法以开关此效果。\n\n这是可怕的鲜血星星之眼。只有陷入永恒黑暗的人，才能召唤这一图腾，能够使其恢复视力。尽是怨恨和饥渴的视景，展现的是在无尽的掠夺驱动下、充满死难者的世界。"
> 4970:"A sorcery from Eochaid, a land near-forgotten.\n\nConjure tiny thorns to suture wounds together, restoring HP and alleviating bleed build up.\n\nCharge to cast multiple times.\n\nIn the ancient kingdom of Eochaid, sects of warrior-priests would accept blood-tithes from willing and unwilling citizens, believing that the more blood that was spilled would only serve to glorify the Blood Star, the source of all strength.\n"
= 4970:"来自几乎被遗忘的欧赫的魔法。\n\n变出细小的刺来缝合伤口，恢复血量并减缓出血量表积累。\n\n蓄力能连续施放多次。\n\n在古老的欧赫王国，武士暨祭司们接受来自自愿者与非自愿者的血税。他们相信，挥洒的鲜血愈多，鲜血星星——众力量之源——愈会因而显耀。"

Lasts for 1 minute.\n\nEochaid fostered many such rituals, often held as public spectacles meant to exalt the horrifying strength of their god.\n"

> 4990:"An aberrant enchantment of the Blood Star.\nLegendary Enchantment\nIncreases damage of aberrant sorceries by 10%, increases casting speed by 40 and grants immunity to bleed but also lowers your absorption to all damage by 20% and lowers your total stamina by 20%.\n\nThis effect never expires, recast the spell to toggle the effect.\n\n\"With eyes that only peer into the darkness, the looming shape of the crimson eye gazes back unblinking. = 4990:"鲜血星星的异端魔法。\n传说中的法术\n提升10%异端魔法攻击力，提升40点施法速度，并赋予对出血异常状态的免疫，但同时降低20%减伤率，降低20%最大精力。\n\n此效果永不过期，再次施法以开关此效果。\n\n“我们只看得到黑暗，赫然耸现的深红眼，回望我们，一眨不眨。我们隐匿的伟大星星；让它卸除汝之重担。尚有许多未完之事。你亲手完成之事；你无需见证之事。”"

You also receive a buff that increases your absorption and holy damage you deal by 10% for 30 seconds.\n\nThe inversion of ghostflame retains the transient power of dissipating spirits. \nRather than releasing the energy in the form of rancor or cold flame, the power is diverted to the ritualist. \nSuch a thing would be considered an abomination to the followers of the great phoenix as it prevents the eventual rebirth of those souls.\n"
= 5050:"受死之鸟葬仪启发的魔法。\n\n立即杀死你召唤的灵魂并引发巨大的灵火爆炸，造成圣属性伤害并积累冻伤量表。\n当召唤灵魂死亡时，你会恢复所有血量、专注值和精力。\n你还会得到一个buff，使你的减伤率和圣属性攻击力提高10%，持续30秒。\n\n反转的灵火保留了能够驱散灵魂的、转瞬即逝的力量。\n这并非以怨魂或冰冷灵火的形式释放力量，而是将力量转移至施术者本身。\n伟大凤凰的追随者对此深恶痛绝——那些灵魂因此而无法抵达最终的重生。"
> 5060:"A sorcery inspired by the funerary rites of the Deathbirds.\n\nEnvelop the caster, all allies and summons in ghostflame. Any nearby enemy will take holy damage and frostbite build-up.\nLasts 40 seconds.\n\nA small portion of the funeral ritual of the Deathbirds, this sorcery has been repurposed by many heretical necromancers, turning them and their wayward spirits into walking weapons.\n"
= 5060:"受死之鸟葬仪启发的魔法。\n\n将施法者、所有友军和召唤物包围在灵火中。对附近任何敌人造成圣属性伤害和冻伤量表积累。\n持续40秒。\n\n这是死之鸟葬仪的一小部分。许多异端死灵术士将这种魔法加以改动，令自身、以及难以驾驭的召唤灵化作行走的武器。"
> 5061:"Sorcery of the servants of Death.\n\nViolently rip an enemy’s soul from their body as a projectile that moves toward the caster. The enemy instantly becomes stunned. \nWhen the soul is absorbed, the caster becomes drained of all stamina for a few seconds and loses all remaining FP. \n\nIf the caster is affected by the Phoenix of Death sorcery, this spell will replenish the Death Ward effect of that spell if Death Ward is not currently active.\n"
= 5061:"侍奉死亡的人物施展的魔法。\n\n猛烈地将敌人的灵魂从他们的身体中撕裂出来，并以飞弹的形式向施法者移动。敌人会被立刻击倒。\n当灵魂被吸收时，施法者在几秒钟内耗尽所有精力，并失去所有剩余的专注值。\n\n如果施法者受到死之凤凰魔法的影响，且死亡之盾失效，该法术会补充死亡之盾的效果。"

= 5250:"古代史东薇尔的烈风召唤者使用的魔法。\n用于武器的法术\n强化右手的武器，附加物理属性攻击力。持续90秒。\n这个魔法可以走动施放。\n\n旧史东薇尔的骑士经常在战斗中使用这些技艺，因为任何尊奉其信条的成员，都必须对元素力量充满热忱。\n这种热忱致使他们最终被当作异端流放。"
> 5260:"An enchantment employed by the elders of Stormveil Castle.\nSignature Enchantment\nInfuse your body with the essence of air, causing the caster to automatically sprint with no stamina use, also dramatically increases stamina recovery, increases casting speed by 40, prevents fall damage and makes you not stagger after falling. \nLasts for 1 minute.\n\nOne of the earliest stable iterations of air infusions that affect the sorcerer’s body. Earlier versions of such practices were dangerous as failed attempts could lead to vaporization.\n\n \n\n"
= 5260:"史东薇尔长老使用的魔法。\n标志性法术\n给身体注入风的精华，使施法者在不使用精力的情况下自动冲刺，也显著提升精力恢复，提升40点施法速度，并防止坠落伤害和坠落产生的硬直。\n持续1分钟。\n\n最早一批能注入大气之力、影响魔法师身体，且具有稳定效果的法术之一。早期的尝试都相当危险，失败可能导致躯体气化。"
> 5261:"An enchantment employed by the elders of Stormveil Castle.\nDefensive Enchantment\nAlter the essence of your physical form into vapors causing the stamina cost of attacks to be decreased by 25%, the FP cost of sorceries to be decreased by 15% and your physical absorption to be increased by 15%. \nLasts for 2 minutes.\n\nA derivative of the Cloud Form enchantment, this technique became invaluable in the great conflict against the force of the Erdtree. \n\n \n\n"
= 5261:"史东薇尔长老使用的魔法。\n防御性法术\n将自身物质形态的本质转化为气态，降低15%攻击精力消耗、15%魔法专注值消耗，提升25%物理减伤率。\n持续2分钟。\n\n云形魔法的衍生，在与黄金树势力的战争中变得非常有用。"
> 5270:"A sorcery used by the Stormcallers of ancient Stormveil.\n\nLaunches a projectile of air at foes. Upon impact, the enemy will be affected by a curse that greatly inhibits their breathing. \nDeals continuous damage over its duration, causes affected enemies to deal 15% less damage, lowers their ability to block attacks and lowers their posture. \nLasts for 80 seconds.\n\nMasters of attrition warfare, the knights of old Stormveil stood as bastions on the battlefield, employing spells that could bring enemy troops to the point of exhaustion even before the battle was joined.\n\n \n\n"
= 5270:"古代史东薇尔的烈风召唤者使用的魔法。\n\n向敌人发射气体飞弹。一旦被击中，敌人将受到诅咒的影响，极大地抑制他们的呼吸。\n在持续时间内造成持续伤害，使受影响的敌人降低15%攻击力，降低防御能力并降低强韧度。\n持续80秒。\n\n作为消耗战的大师，旧史东薇尔的骑士们如堡垒般屹立于战场。他们施展的法术，甚至不等战斗打响，就能令敌方士兵陷入疲乏。"

For every stack of Current consumed you gain damage negation and HP regeneration for a maximum of 20% damage negation and 30 HP per second at 15 stacks of Current.\n\nFor those who live eternal, sleep is likened to death. In the time of the mighty Dragonlord, the Ancients vowed to never slumber while in the service of their lord, lest they be forgotten.\n"
= 6993:"传说中的法术\n古龙的鳞片可以时间，此为其中一种展现。\n\n呼唤古龙的力量，使龙之活力充盈全身，持续1分钟。期间每消耗1点“电流”，就会增加减伤率以及每秒恢复血量。最大可消耗15点“电流”，增加20%减伤率，每秒恢复30点血量。\n\n对永生不朽的存在而言，沉眠与死亡别无二致。强大的龙王尚在的时代，古龙们曾立下绝不在侍奉君王时沉眠的誓言，因其恐惧自身会被遗忘。"

< 210000:"Ashen remains in which spirits yet dwell.\nUse to summon the spirit of a winged misbegotten.\n\nA spirit with the aspect of wings which takes flight to loose arrows from its bow. The misbegotten are held to be a punishment for making contact with the Crucible, and from birth they are treated as slaves, or worse."
> 210000:"Ashen remains in which spirits yet dwell.\nUse to summon three winged misbegotten spirits.\n\nSpirits with the aspect of wings which takes flight to loose arrows from its bow. The misbegotten are held to be a punishment for making contact with the Crucible, and from birth they are treated as slaves, or worse."
- 210000:"寄宿着灵魂的骨灰。\n能召唤带翼混种的灵魂。\n\n拥有翅膀百相，边飞边射箭的灵魂。\n混种的诞生，据说是接触熔炉所降下的惩罚。\n因此他们生来就是奴隶，被称为玷污者。"

< 235000:"Ashen remains in which spirits yet dwell.\nUse to summon the spirit of a rotten stray.\n\nSpirit of a stray dog corrupted by the scarlet rot.\nThough it is only a small creature, it is as violent as it is nimble, and its fangs fester with poisonous rot."
> 235000:"Ashen remains in which spirits yet dwell.\nUse to summon two rotten stray spirits.\n\nSpirits of stray dogs corrupted by the scarlet rot.\nThough they are only small creatures, they are as violent as they are nimble, and their fangs fester with poisonous rot."

- 235005:"寄宿着灵魂的骨灰。\n能召唤腐败野狗的灵魂。\n\n受到猩红腐败侵蚀的野狗灵魂。\n体型偏小，动作迅速，性格十分凶暴。\n那口骯脏的牙布满了腐败的毒素。"

< 245000:"Ashen remains in which spirits yet dwell.\nUse to summon the spirits of five miranda sprouts.\nSummoning consumes HP rather than FP.\n\nSpirits of sweet little miranda flowers, carnivorous blossoms that feed upon human flesh. They creep slowly, scattering toxic pollen.\nVulnerable to fire—do take care of the little darlings."
> 245000:"Ashen remains in which spirits yet dwell.\nUse to summon the spirits of five miranda sprouts.\n\nSpirits of sweet little miranda flowers, carnivorous blossoms that feed upon human flesh. They creep slowly, scattering toxic pollen.\nVulnerable to fire—do take care of the little darlings."
- 245000:"寄宿着灵魂的骨灰。\n能召唤５只小米兰达的灵魂。\n召唤时不消耗专注值，而是血量。\n\n会吃人的花，米兰达之花──\n它娇小可爱的幼株群灵魂。\n会缓慢蠕动，努力释放有毒花粉。\n但是不耐火，要特别小心。"
= 245000:"寄宿着灵魂的骨灰。\n能召唤５只小米兰达的灵魂。\n\n会吃人的花，米兰达之花──\n它娇小可爱的幼株群灵魂。\n会缓慢蠕动，努力释放有毒花粉。\n但是不耐火，要特别小心。"
< 245001:"Ashen remains in which spirits yet dwell.\nUse to summon the spirits of five miranda sprouts.\nSummoning consumes HP rather than FP.\n\nSpirits of sweet little miranda flowers, carnivorous blossoms that feed upon human flesh. They creep slowly, scattering toxic pollen.\nVulnerable to fire—do take care of the little darlings."

< 246000:"Ashen remains in which spirits yet dwell.\nUse to summon the spirits of three little living jars.\nSummoning consumes HP rather than FP.\n\nThese reckless spirits sacrifice themselves to vanquish their summoner's foes, and explode upon death.\nThough their bravery is admirable, their explosions can harm friend as well as foe, and they will also immediately explode on contact with fire.\n\n\"Tell the others—tell them how brightly a fire jar burns.\""
> 246000:"Ashen remains in which spirits yet dwell.\nUse to summon the spirits of three little living jars.\n\nThese reckless spirits sacrifice themselves to vanquish their summoner's foes, and explode upon death.\nThough their bravery is admirable, their explosions can harm friend as well as foe, and they will also immediately explode on contact with fire.\n\n\"Tell the others—tell them how brightly a fire jar burns.\""
- 246000:"寄宿着灵魂的骨灰。\n能召唤３名小型活壶的灵魂。\n召唤时不消耗专注值，而是血量。\n\n会对敌人展开特攻，死亡时会爆炸，\n一群视死如归的灵魂。\n表现得很勇敢，但爆炸也会波及我方。\n碰触到火焰会立刻爆炸。\n\n\u3000帮我们转告给故乡的大家吧──\n\u3000我们火焰壶，表现的点点滴滴……"

- 246005:"寄宿着灵魂的骨灰。\n能召唤３名小型活壶的灵魂。\n召唤时不消耗专注值，而是血量。\n\n会对敌人展开特攻，死亡时会爆炸，\n一群视死如归的灵魂。\n表现得很勇敢，但爆炸也会波及我方。\n碰触到火焰会立刻爆炸。\n\n\u3000帮我们转告给故乡的大家吧──\n\u3000我们火焰壶，表现的点点滴滴……"
